HTTP to RBAC Verb Mapping\\nThe mapping occurs in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go` via the `toDiscoveryKubeVerb` map:\\n- POST → create\\n- GET → get  \\n- PUT → update\\n- PATCH → patch\\n- DELETE → delete\\n- LIST → list\\n- WATCH/WATCHLIST → watch\\n- DELETECOLLECTION → deletecollection\\n- CONNECT → (internal, not exposed in discovery)\\n\\nThis mapping is set during API resource handler registration in the `Install()` method (line 192) and `registerResourceHandlers()` method.\\n\\n### 3. Request Processing Chain\\nWhen a request arrives:\\n1. `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/request/requestinfo.go` (`GetAPIRequestInfo()`) parses the HTTP method and URL to determine the verb\\n2. The verb is stored in the RequestInfo structure\\n3. `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/authorization.go` (`WithAuthorization()` middleware) is invoked\\n4. Authorization attributes are extracted via `GetAuthorizerAttributes()` which includes the verb from RequestInfo\\n5. The RBAC authorizer (`plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/rbac.go`) evaluates if the rule allows the verb\\n\\n### 4. Verb Matching in RBAC\\nThe core verb matching logic is in `pkg/apis/rbac/v1/evaluation_helpers.go`:\\n- `VerbMatches()` checks if a PolicyRule's verbs include the requested verb or \\\"*\\\"\\n- `APIGroupMatches()`, `ResourceMatches()`, `ResourceNameMatches()`, `NonResourceURLMatches()` handle other rule dimensions\\n- Rules are combined with OR logic (any matching rule allows the request)\\n\\n### 5. Handler Implementation\\nEach RBAC verb has a corresponding REST handler:\\n- Create: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/create.go` → `CreateResource()`\\n- Get: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/get.go` → `GetResource()`\\n- List: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/get.go` (via LIST action)\\n- Watch: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/watch.go`\\n- Update: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/update.go` → `UpdateResource()`\\n- Patch: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/patch.go` → `PatchResource()`\\n- Delete: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/delete.go` → `DeleteResource()`\\n- DeleteCollection: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/delete.go` → `DeleteCollection()`\\n- Connect: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/rest.go` → `ConnectResource()`\\n\\nHandlers are conditionally registered based on which REST storage interfaces the resource implements (Getter, Creater, Lister, Updater, Patcher, GracefulDeleter, CollectionDeleter, Watcher, Connecter).\\n\\n### 6. Storage Interface Abstraction\\nThe `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest/rest.go` defines interfaces that storage implementations must satisfy to enable specific verbs. Each interface maps to a verb capability:\\n- Getter → get verb\\n- Lister → list verb\\n- Watcher → watch verb\\n- Creater/NamedCreater → create verb\\n- Updater → update verb\\n- Patcher → patch verb\\n- GracefulDeleter → delete verb\\n- CollectionDeleter → deletecollection verb\\n- Connecter → connect verb\\n\\n### 7.
